Description: Validate successful voluntary booking change requiring additional payment.

Preconditions:
• Passenger: Tom Smith
• PNR: AC7K9L
• No SSR, baggage, group, ACV, OAL

Given Tom Smith has Air Canada booking PNR AC7K9L for flight AC104 Toronto → Vancouver on 20-Jun-2026
And Tom opens the Air Canada chatbot
Then the chatbot displays greeting:
"Hello! I will be your virtual assistant today. I can assist you in English or French. Which language would you prefer to use today?
Then user selects English
Then an alert information is displayed " Please note  that by using this service, you will interact with an automated chatbot which uses AI to answer your questions and requests. Your personal information will be used to identify and authenticate you, to answer your request, and for other purposes detailed in the Privacy Notice."
Then chatbot ask "How can I help you today?"
And the user responds: "I'd like to change my flight"
And the chatbot displays legal disclaimer "Please note that the assessment and decision regarding your request will be made through an automated decision making process. To process your request, you'll need your booking reference and the full name associated to the booking. Dependingon the changes you select, payment may be required. Please have access to youy preferred method of payment. Would you like to get started?" 
And Tom accepts the disclaimer

Preconditions:
• Passenger: David Brown
• PNR: DB5P7Q
• Outbound on lower fare (change fee applied)

Given David Brown has booking PNR DB5P7Q from Montreal to Calgary
And David opens the Air Canada chatbot
Then the chatbot displays greeting:
""Hello! I will be your virtual assistant today. I can assist you in English or French. Which language would you prefer to use today?
Then user selects English
Then an alert information is displayed "" Please note  that by using this service, you will interact with an automated chatbot which uses AI to answer your questions and requests. Your personal information will be used to identify and authenticate you, to answer your request, and for other purposes detailed in the Privacy Notice.""
Then chatbot ask ""How can I help you today?""
And the user responds: "I'd like to change my flight"
And the chatbot displays legal disclaimer ""Please note that the assessment and decision regarding your request will be made through an automated decision making process. To process your request, you'll need your booking reference and the full name associated to the booking. Dependingon the changes you select, payment may be required. Please have access to youy preferred method of payment. Would you like to get started?"" 
And David accepts the disclaimer

IDENTIFICATION:
Then the chatbot responds:
""I can definitely help you with that. To start I'll just need to know some information to be able to process your request and identify you.""
And the chatbot responds:
""Please provide your full name exactly as it appears on your ticket, including any middle names if applicable.""
And the user provides ""David Brown""
Then the chatbot responds:
""Thanks, David! And, what is your booking reference number?""
And the user provides ""PNR DB5P7Q""
Then the chatbot searches Trip Tracer for PNR DB5P7Q
And Trip Tracer returns: PNR FOUND (Auth Flow 1)

AUTHENTICATION:
Then the chatbot responds:
""To keep your account secure and assist you further, I'll need to verify your identity. I'll do this by sending a one-time verification code to either your email or phone number on file. Where would you like to receive it?""
And the chatbot displays options:
• Email: d***@gmail.com
• Phone: +1***567
And the user selects ""Email: d***@gmail.com""
Then the chatbot responds:
""I've sent a verification code to your email, please enter it within 15 minutes of receiving it.""
And the user provides the OTP code ""591837""
Then the chatbot validates the OTP code → CORRECT (attempt 1 of 5)
Then the chatbot responds:
""Your verification was successful. Let's proceed to the next step.""

Given Lisa Park has Air Canada booking PNR LP6N3R for flight AC200 Montreal → Vancouver in Economy cabin 
And Lisa opens the Air Canada chatbot
Then the chatbot displays greeting:
""Hello! I will be your virtual assistant today. I can assist you in English or French. Which language would you prefer to use today?
Then user selects English
Then an alert information is displayed "" Please note  that by using this service, you will interact with an automated chatbot which uses AI to answer your questions and requests. Your personal information will be used to identify and authenticate you, to answer your request, and for other purposes detailed in the Privacy Notice.""

And the user responds: ""I'd like to change my flight""
And the chatbot displays legal disclaimer ""Please note that the assessment and decision regarding your request will be made through an automated decision making process. Description: Validate that when a customer expresses intent to downgrade their cabin (e.g., Business → Economy) during the cabin change flow, the chatbot detects the downgrade request and proceeds for live agent hand-off.

Preconditions:
• Passenger: Samantha Smith
• PNR: SM8D4K
• Original booking: Business class cabin
• Customer is VOL eligible
• Customer is authenticated
• Customer has selected "Upgrade my flight" or expressed cabin change intent
• Customer requests a downgrade (lower cabin than currently booked)

Given Samantha Smith has Air Canada booking PNR "SM8D4K" for flight AC654 Toronto → London in Business class cabin
And Samantha opens the Air Canada chatbot
Then the chatbot displays greeting:
""Hello! I will be your virtual assistant today. I can assist you in English or French. Which language would you prefer to use today?
Then user selects English
Then an alert information is displayed "" Please note  that by using this service, you will interact with an automated chatbot which uses AI to answer your questions and requests. Then user will be handed off to a live agent

📋 Raw Action / Description
Validate that multi-passenger bookings are handled when all passengers are changed together. 
Preconditions: 
•Passengers: Anna White, Brian White 
•PNR: AW4R8M 
•Two passengers on same PNR 
•No split passenger records

Given Anna White and Brian White have booking PNR AW4R8M for flight AC500 Ottawa → Vancouver 
And Anna opens the Air Canada chatbot
Then the chatbot displays greeting:
""Hello! I will be your virtual assistant today. I can assist you in English or French. Which language would you prefer to use today?
Then user selects English
Then an alert information is displayed "" Please note  that by using this service, you will interact with an automated chatbot which uses AI to answer your questions and requests. Your personal information will be used to identify and authenticate you, to answer your request, and for other purposes detailed in the Privacy Notice.""
Then chatbot ask ""How can I help you today?""
And the user responds: ""I'd like to change my flight""
And the chatbot displays legal disclaimer ""Please note that the assessment and decision regarding your request will be made through an automated decision making process. To process your request, you'll need your booking reference and the full name associated to the booking. Dependingon the changes you select, payment may be required. Please have access to youy preferred method of payment. Would you like to get started?"" 
And Anna accepts the disclaimer

IDENTIFICATION:
Then the chatbot responds:
""I can definitely help you with that. To start I'll just need to know some information to be able to process your request and identify you.""
And the chatbot responds:
""Please provide your full name exactly as it appears on your ticket, including any middle names if applicable.""
And the user provides ""Anna White""
Then the chatbot responds:
""Thanks, Anna! And, what is your booking reference number?""
And the user provides ""PNR AW4R8M""
Then the chatbot searches Trip Tracer for PNR AW4R8M
And Trip Tracer returns: PNR FOUND (Auth Flow 1)

AUTHENTICATION:
Then the chatbot responds:

• Email: a***@gmail.com
• Phone: +1***567
And the user selects ""Email: a***@gmail.com""

Then the chatbot responds:
""Your verification was successful. Let's proceed to the next step.""

Description: Validate the complete end-to-end happy path for voluntary booking change for 2 ADT + 1 CHD + 1 INF (lap infant).

Preconditions:
• Michael Carter (ADT), Sarah Carter (ADT), Emma Carter (CHD age 7), Baby Carter (INF age 10 months)
• PNR: MC4R8K
• Flight: AC500 YYZ → YVR
• Ticket stock: 014
• Booking source: ACB
• Fare: Flex Economy
• SSR: INFT only (non-blocking)
• Not checked in, no baggage

Given passengers Michael Carter, Sarah Carter, Emma Carter, and Baby Carter have booking PNR MC4R8K
And Baby Carter is passenger type INF attached to Sarah Carter
And SSR INFT exists and is not blocking
And Michael opens the Air Canada chatbot
Then the chatbot displays greeting:
""Hello! I will be your virtual assistant today. I can assist you in English or French. Which language would you prefer to use today?
Then user selects English

📋 Raw Action / Description
Description: Validate the complete end-to-end happy path for a voluntary booking change on a same-day two-segment one-way itinerary where the passenger is mid-journey at the connecting city.

Preconditions:
• Passenger: Tom Smith (ADT, single passenger)
• PNR: TS6M2P
• Segment 1: AC400 YYZ → YUL — FLOWN, coupon USED
• Segment 2: AC450 YUL → YHZ — UNFLOWN, coupon Open
• Booking source: ACB
• Ticket stock: 014
• Fare: Flex Economy
• No blocking SSRs
• No checked baggage
• Not checked in for Segment 2

Given the user opens the agentic chatbot
Then the chatbot displays greeting (GLOB-01):
"Hello! I will be your virtual assistant today. I can assist you in English or French. Which language would you prefer to use today?"
Then user selects English
Then an alert information is displayed "Please note that by using this service, you will interact with an automated chatbot which uses AI to answer your questions and requests. Your personal information will be used to identify and authenticate you, to answer your request, and for other purposes detailed in the Privacy Notice."

And the user says "I'd like to change my connecting flight"
When the chatbot identifies booking change intent
And the chatbot displays legal disclaimer
And Tom accepts the disclaimer

Description: Validate the complete end-to-end flow when a passenger has completed their entire journey — both segments have been flown (acceptance.status = "BOARDED", coupon = "USED" for both) — and the passenger contacts the chatbot requesting a voluntary booking change.

The system must evaluate eligibility per segment individually. When ALL segments fail eligibility (both are flown), the system must determine that zero segments are eligible for voluntary change.

The chatbot must:
• Acknowledge that the entire itinerary has been completed
• NOT display BCVol-02 options
• NOT proceed to flight selection, seat selection, or payment
• Inform the passenger that no changes are possible
• Offer alternative assistance
• Proceed to End Flow (GLOB-11)

📋 Raw Action / Description
Description: Validate the complete end-to-end flow when a passenger has a same-day two-segment itinerary where Segment 1 (Toronto → Montreal) has been flown and Segment 2 (Montreal → Halifax) is unflown but the passenger is already checked in for it.

When a passenger checks in for a connecting itinerary, airlines typically check in for ALL remaining segments at once.

At BCVol-03, the system checks if any segment is checked in. If yes, chatbot directs passenger to SSCI for check-in cancellation. After customer returns, backend re-verifies via Order Retrieve API (ADD-70).

Preconditions:
• Passenger: Tom Smith (ADT, single passenger)
• PNR: TS6M2P
• Segment 1: AC400 YYZ → YUL — FLOWN
• Segment 2: AC450 YUL → YHZ — CHECKED_IN
• Booking Source: ACB
• Ticket Stock: 014
• No blocking SSRs
• No checked baggage
• Current time: 14-May-2026 12:57 IST
• Segment 2 departure: ~10.5 hours away
